SELECT [d0].[Id], [d0].[Name], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT COUNT(*)
        FROM [DishIngredients] AS [d]
        WHERE [d0].[Id] = [d].[DishId]) > 0 THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, [t].[IngredientId], [t].[Name], [t].[MeasureUnit], [t].[Proportion], [t].[DishId], [t].[Id]
FROM [Dishes] AS [d0]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d1].[IngredientId], [i].[Name], [i].[MeasureUnit], [d1].[Proportion], [d1].[DishId], [i].[Id]
    FROM [DishIngredients] AS [d1]
    INNER JOIN [Ingredients] AS [i] ON [d1].[IngredientId] = [i].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [d0].[Id] = [t].[DishId]
WHERE ([d0].[CompanyId] = @__companyId_0) AND @__companyId_0 IS NOT NULL
ORDER BY [d0].[Id], [t].[DishId], [t].[IngredientId], [t].[Id]

SELECT [d0].[Id], [d0].[Name], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT COUNT(*)
        FROM [DishIngredients] AS [d]
        WHERE [d0].[Id] = [d].[DishId]) > 0 THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, [t].[IngredientId], [t].[Name], [t].[MeasureUnit], [t].[Proportion], [t].[DishId], [t].[Id]
FROM [Dishes] AS [d0]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d1].[IngredientId], [i].[Name], [i].[MeasureUnit], [d1].[Proportion], [d1].[DishId], [i].[Id]
    FROM [DishIngredients] AS [d1]
    INNER JOIN [Ingredients] AS [i] ON [d1].[IngredientId] = [i].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [d0].[Id] = [t].[DishId]
WHERE ([d0].[CompanyId] = @__companyId_0) AND @__companyId_0 IS NOT NULL
ORDER BY [d0].[Id], [t].[DishId], [t].[IngredientId], [t].[Id]

SELECT [d0].[Id], [d0].[Name], CASE
    WHEN (
        SELECT COUNT(*)
        FROM [DishIngredients] AS [d]
        WHERE [d0].[Id] = [d].[DishId]) > 0 THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, [t].[IngredientId], [t].[Name], [t].[MeasureUnit], [t].[Proportion], [t].[DishId], [t].[Id]
FROM [Dishes] AS [d0]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d1].[IngredientId], [i].[Name], [i].[MeasureUnit], [d1].[Proportion], [d1].[DishId], [i].[Id]
    FROM [DishIngredients] AS [d1]
    INNER JOIN [Ingredients] AS [i] ON [d1].[IngredientId] = [i].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [d0].[Id] = [t].[DishId]
WHERE ([d0].[CompanyId] = @__companyId_0) AND @__companyId_0 IS NOT NULL
ORDER BY [d0].[Id], [t].[DishId], [t].[IngredientId], [t].[Id]
